--
-- Table structure for table `lu_manufacturers`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `lu_manufacturers`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `lu_manufacturers` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'primary key - ccr tracks manufacturer of medications',
  `displayText` varchar(45) NOT NULL COMMENT 'name of manufacture - Pfizer, Bayer, etc.',
  `description` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'short desc about manufacture - e.g. manufacture located in Midwest producing generic version of drugs',
  `contactName` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'if provided, contact for manufacture\ne.g Mary Smith',
  `addressType` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'we shouldn''t have to store multiple addresses, will start with one. \ne.g. Headquarters, New England Division etc',
  `line1` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'address line 1 e.g. 123 Main Street',
  `line2` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Address line 2 e.g. Suite 123',
  `city` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Boston',
  `state` varchar(2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'MA',
  `zip` varchar(15) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '02116',
  `country` varchar(25) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'USA',
  `phone1Type` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'type of phone - Toll Free, Main Office',
  `phone1` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '617-123-4567',
  `phone2Type` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'regular office number, 1st floor, etc',
  `phone2` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '123-456-7890',
  `fax` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'fax number for manufacture - 1234567890',
  `isCustom` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'0' COMMENT 'This field tracks look up item and flags it as 1 if it is a custom field that should not be a general option. 1 for True, 0 for False',
  `status` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'1' COMMENT 'This field is 1 if it is available to general public and in use.  It is set to 0 when it is no longer available as a choice to users. 1 for True, 0 for False',
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT 'This is the date that the record was added to UT',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;

CREATE TABLE `message_fammemmedicalconditions` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `transactionInId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `sourceId` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'This is the id that the message source might have assigned to the record. For example, CCR components always has a CCRDataObjectId',
  `sourceDateType` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'The date type that the is provided with the record. It can be a date range, exact date, approximate date range, approximately age range, age range, verification date etc. ',
  `sourceDate` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'The date that the is provided with the record. e.g. exact time - Nov 11, 2011 11:11AM, age range - age 19-25',
  `familyMemberId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'The id from message_FamilyMembers table.',
  `conditionTypeId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Id from lu_MedicalConditonTypes',
  `conditionId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id from lu_MedicalConditons table',
  `conditionDate` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'The date that the is provided with the record for the condition. It could be different from SourceDate as sourceDate can be a range of when the patient is follow and conditionDate is when this medical condition happened. It can be a date range, exact date, approximate date range, approximately age range, age range, etc. e.g. exact time - Nov 11, 2011 11:11AM, age range - age 19-25',
  `conditionStatusId` int(11) DEFAULT '1' COMMENT 'id from lu_MedicalConditionStatuses table',

  `codingVersion` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'the version of the coding system etc. ICD-9CM''s version might be 2004',
  `comments` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'any additional information for the medical condition.',
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT 'This is the date that the record was added to UT',

  KEY `fmmcFMId_idx` (`familyMemberId`),
  KEY `FMM_tranId_idx` (`transactionInId`),

--
-- Table structure for table `message_medications`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `message_medications`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `message_medications` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `transactionInId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `sourceId` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'This is the id that the message source might have assigned to the record. For example, CCR components always has a CCRDataObjectId',
  `sourceDateType` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'The date type that the is provided with the record. It can be a date range, exact date, approximate date range, approximately age range, age range, verification date etc. ',
  `sourceDate` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'The date that the is provided with the record. e.g. exact time - Nov 11, 2011 11:11AM, age range - age 19-25',
  `manufacturerId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id from lu_Manufacturers',
  `brandNameId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id from lu_brandName',
  `medicationId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'look up from lu_Medications',
  `quantity` float DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'How much in total a patient should get of this medication e.g. 30',
  `quantityUnit` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'How much in total a patient should get of this medication e.g. capsules',
  `dosage` float DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'how much a patient should take each time e.g. 1',
  `dosageUnit` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'how much a patient should take each time e.g. capsule',
  `duration` float DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'how long should a patient take this  - e.g. 30',
  `durationUnit` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Unit of how long should a patient take this  - e.g. days',
  `frequency` float DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'how often should a patient take this  - e.g. 1',
  `frequencyUnit` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'The unit of often should a patient take this  - e.g. day',
  `directions` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'more specific directions - Stop taking if symptoms are gone.',
  `medGeneralStatusId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'past, current, future, etc.',
  `medOrder` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'If there are multiple medications for a message, specify the order medications of if needed.',
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT 'This is the date that the record was added to UT',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `medFK_idx` (`medicationId`),
  KEY `medStatusFK_idx` (`medGeneralStatusId`),
  KEY `meDManuFK_idx` (`manufacturerId`),
  KEY `medBrandNameFK_idx` (`brandNameId`),
  KEY `med_tranId_idx` (`transactionInId`),
  CONSTRAINT `medBrandFK` FOREIGN KEY (`brandNameId`) REFERENCES `lu_brandnames` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `medFK` FOREIGN KEY (`medicationId`) REFERENCES `lu_medications` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `meDManuFK` FOREIGN KEY (`manufacturerId`) REFERENCES `lu_manufacturers` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `med_tranId` FOREIGN KEY (`transactionInId`) REFERENCES `transactionin` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

--
-- Table structure for table `message_patientaddresses`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `message_patientaddresses`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `message_patientaddresses` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'primary key for table',
  `transactionInId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `type` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'The type could be vacation, home, office, etc.',
  `line1` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Address line 1 - e.g. 123 Main Street',
  `line2` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Address line 2 - e.g. Suite 123',
  `city` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'city - e.g. Beantown',
  `state` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'State - e.g. MA',
  `postalCode` varchar(15) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'zipcode - 02116',
  `countyId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `country` varchar(25) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. USA',
  `phoneType1` varchar(25) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id related to lu_PhoneTypes Tables',
  `phone1` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. 617-111-1111',
  `phoneType2` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id related to lu_PhoneTypes Tables',
  `phone2` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. 123-456-7890\n',
  `fax` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. 857-123-4567',
  `addressOrder` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'order of address importance - e.g. 1, 2, 3',
  `status` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'pending, current, future, etc.',
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT 'This is the date that the record was added to UT',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `coutyFK_idx` (`countyId`),
  KEY `paPhone1FK_idx` (`phoneType1`),
  KEY `paPhoneType2FK_idx` (`phoneType2`),
  KEY `padd_tranId_idx` (`transactionInId`),
  CONSTRAINT `coutyFK` FOREIGN KEY (`countyId`) REFERENCES `lu_counties` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `padd_tranId` FOREIGN KEY (`transactionInId`) REFERENCES `transactionin` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;

--
-- Table structure for table `message_patients`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `message_patients`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `message_patients` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'primary key for patient, it will serve as our system''s patient Id',
  `transactionInId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `sourcePatientId` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Id assigned to patient by source system - e.g Pat148R-2KD-BOS',
  `prefix` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. Mr, Dr., Ms, Sir, Princess, Knight, etc',
  `firstName` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. John',
  `middleName` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g Joshua',
  `lastName` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. Doe',
  `suffix` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. Jr, III, IV etc.',
  `dob` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Patient''s date of birth 1-1-1912',
  `genderId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Look up value from lu_Genders. Look up field is int and not free hand field because we should have some limits to some fields as what the user can type.  We will add it to our look up table if something creative comes up.  It is also a repetitive field, using int will take up less space and faster when it comes to indexing\nSample equivalent values are - male, female, unknown, transgender, etc.',
  `raceId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Look up Id from lu_Races - equivalent values could be Asian, White, Black, etc.',
  `hispanicId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id from lu_Hispanics\nSample look up values are Yes, No, Not Reported',
  `primaryLanguageId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Id from lu_Languages - Sample look up values - English, Spanish, Polish, Mandarin (Chinese), Cantonese (Chinese) etc.',
  `englishProficient` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'can be Yes, No, Unknown...\nWe wi\nso changing it to varchar',
  `maritalStatusId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'look up from lu_MartialStatuses - Sample look up values are - Single, Married, Divorced, Not Reported, etc.',
  `initialContraceptiveId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `initialNoContraceptiveId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `email` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. test@test.com',
  `additonalContactNumber` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  `url` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. http://test.com',
  `occupation` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  `guardianName` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'name of guardian - Jane Doe, John Smith',
  `emergencyContact` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Name of emergency contact - Jane Doe',
  `emergencyTel` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '123-456-7890',
  `patientStatusId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id from lu_PatientStatuses - Could be equivalent int value of active, pending, future, expired, etc.',
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT 'This is the date that the record was added to UT',
  `race` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `genderFK_idx` (`genderId`),
  KEY `raceFK_idx` (`raceId`),
  KEY `lauguageFK_idx` (`primaryLanguageId`),
  KEY `martialStatusFK_idx` (`maritalStatusId`),
  KEY `patientStatuses_idx` (`patientStatusId`),
  KEY `hispanicFK_idx` (`hispanicId`),
  KEY `contraFK_idx` (`initialContraceptiveId`),
  KEY `transFK_idx` (`transactionInId`),
  CONSTRAINT `contraFK` FOREIGN KEY (`initialContraceptiveId`) REFERENCES `lu_contraceptives` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `genderFK` FOREIGN KEY (`genderId`) REFERENCES `lu_genders` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `hispanicFK` FOREIGN KEY (`hispanicId`) REFERENCES `lu_hispanics` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `lauguageFK` FOREIGN KEY (`primaryLanguageId`) REFERENCES `lu_languages` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `martialStatusFK` FOREIGN KEY (`maritalStatusId`) REFERENCES `lu_martialstatuses` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `patientStatuses` FOREIGN KEY (`patientStatusId`) REFERENCES `lu_patientstatuses` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `raceFK` FOREIGN KEY (`raceId`) REFERENCES `lu_races` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `transFK` FOREIGN KEY (`transactionInId`) REFERENCES `transactionin` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;

--
-- Table structure for table `message_payers`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `message_payers`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `message_payers` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `transactionInId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `sourceId` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'This is the id that the message source might have assigned to the record. For example, CCR components always has a CCRDataObjectId',
  `sourceDateType` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'The date type that the is provided with the record. It can be a date range, exact date, approximate date range, approximately age range, age range, verification date etc. ',
  `sourceDate` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'The date that the is provided with the record. e.g. exact time - Nov 11, 2011 11:11AM, age range - age 19-25',
  `payerTypeId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Id from lu_Payers table',
  `issuer` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Issuer of this payment type - e.g. Blue Cross Blue Shield',
  `groupNumber` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Group Number for this payer type - XXP12345',
  `planNumber` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'The plan number for this payment type - planACBDFER123',
  `policyHolder` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Name of the policy holder - John Smith',
  `relationToPatient` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Relation to patient - self, spouse, father, etc.',
  `startDate` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Payment method start date',
  `endDate` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Payment method end date',
  `status` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'if the payment is active, no longer active, etc.',
  `payerOrder` int(11) DEFAULT '1' COMMENT 'payment order, 1, 2, 3 etc.',
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT 'This is the date that the record was added to UT',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `payerIdFK_idx` (`payerTypeId`),
  KEY `payers_tranId_idx` (`transactionInId`),
  CONSTRAINT `payerIdFK` FOREIGN KEY (`payerTypeId`) REFERENCES `lu_payertypes` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,

--
-- Table structure for table `rel_messagetypedatatranslations`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `rel_messagetypedatatranslations`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `rel_messagetypedatatranslations` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `messageTypeId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `fieldId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `crosswalkId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `processOrder` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `messageTypeId_idx` (`messageTypeId`),
  KEY `cwId_idx` (`crosswalkId`),
  KEY `msgFieldId_idx` (`fieldId`),
  CONSTRAINT `cwId` FOREIGN KEY (`crosswalkId`) REFERENCES `crosswalks` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `msgFieldId` FOREIGN KEY (`fieldId`) REFERENCES `messagetypeformfields` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `msgTypeId` FOREIGN KEY (`messageTypeId`) REFERENCES `messagetypes` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;

  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `transportId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `IP` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  `directory` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `username` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  `password` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  `method` smallint(6) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '1 = Push\n2 = Get',
  `port` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `protocol` varchar(45) DEFAULT 'FTP',
  `certification` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `transportId_idx` (`transportId`),
  CONSTRAINT `transportId` FOREIGN KEY (`transportId`) REFERENCES `configurationtransportdetails` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION

  `configId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `statusId` int(11) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Id from lu_TransactionStatuses\n\nCould be Rejected\nPending\nReleased\nError,\netc',
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `transactionTargetId` int(11) DEFAULT '0',

  `messageStatus` int(11) DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '1 = Open\n2 = Closed',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `statusFK_idx` (`statusId`),
  KEY `configIdFK_idx` (`configId`),
  KEY `batchFK_idx` (`batchId`),
  KEY `batchAndIdIdx` (`id`,`batchId`),
  KEY `idAndStatusId` (`id`,`statusId`),
  CONSTRAINT `batchFK` FOREIGN KEY (`batchId`) REFERENCES `batchuploads` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `statusFK` FOREIGN KEY (`statusId`) REFERENCES `lu_processstatus` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

--
-- Table structure for table `transactionouterrors`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `transactionouterrors`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `transactionouterrors` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `BatchDownloadId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `transactionTargetId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `configId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `fieldNo` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `required` bit(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  `errorId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `cwId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `macroId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `validationTypeId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `stackTrace` text,
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `configFFIdFK_idx` (`fieldNo`),
  KEY `FKErrorId_idx` (`errorId`),
  KEY `validationTypeFKOut_idx` (`validationTypeId`),
  KEY `cwId_idx` (`cwId`),
  KEY `macroId_idx` (`macroId`),
  CONSTRAINT `cwIdFK` FOREIGN KEY (`cwId`) REFERENCES `crosswalks` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `errorIdFK` FOREIGN KEY (`errorId`) REFERENCES `lu_errorcodes` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `FKErrorId` FOREIGN KEY (`errorId`) REFERENCES `lu_errorcodes` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `macroIdFK` FOREIGN KEY (`macroId`) REFERENCES `macro_names` (`ID`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `validationTypeFKOut` FOREIGN KEY (`validationTypeId`) REFERENCES `ref_validationtypes` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;

--
-- Table structure for table `transactiontarget`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `transactiontarget`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `transactiontarget` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `batchUploadId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `transactionInId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `batchDLId` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `configId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `statusId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `statusTime` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `internalStatusId` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `ttargetInFK_idx` (`transactionInId`),
  KEY `targetBatchId_idx` (`batchUploadId`),
  KEY `ttargetStatusId_idx` (`statusId`),
  KEY `ttargetConfigIdFK_idx` (`configId`),
  KEY `IdAndBatchIndex` (`id`,`batchDLId`),
  KEY `UploadInfo` (`transactionInId`,`batchUploadId`),
  KEY `DLInfo` (`batchDLId`,`id`,`configId`),
  CONSTRAINT `targetBatchId` FOREIGN KEY (`batchUploadId`) REFERENCES `batchuploads` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `ttargetConfigIdFK` FOREIGN KEY (`configId`) REFERENCES `configurations` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `ttargetInFK` FOREIGN KEY (`transactionInId`) REFERENCES `transactionin` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `ttargetStatusId` FOREIGN KEY (`statusId`) REFERENCES `lu_processstatus` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;

-- Dumping data for table `transactiontarget`
--

LOCK TABLES `transactiontarget` WRITE;
/*!40000 ALTER TABLE `transactiontarget` DISABLE KEYS */;
/*!40000 ALTER TABLE `transactiontarget` ENABLE KEYS */;
UNLOCK TABLES;

-- Table structure for table `users`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `users`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `users` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `status` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'1',
  `orgId` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `firstName` varchar(55) NOT NULL,
  `lastName` varchar(55) NOT NULL,
  `username` varchar(15) NOT NULL,
  `password` varchar(15) DEFAULT NULL,
  `roleId` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '2',
  `mainContact` smallint(6) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '0 = Not a Main Contact\n1 = Primary Contact\n2 = Secondary Contact',
  `sendEmailAlert` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'0' COMMENT '0 = No Email Alerts\n1 = Send Email Alerts',
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `email` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `userType` smallint(6) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '1 = Manager\n2 = Staff Member',
  `deliverAuthority` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'0',
  `editAuthority` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'0',
  `createAuthority` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'0',
  `cancelAuthority` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'0',
  `resetCode` varchar(8) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `userOrgId_idx` (`orgId`),
  KEY `userRoleId_idx` (`roleId`),
  CONSTRAINT `userRoleId` FOREIGN KEY (`roleId`) REFERENCES `userroles` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `usersOrgId` FOREIGN KEY (`orgId`) REFERENCES `organizations` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=23 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` FUNCTION `strSplit`(x varchar(255), delim varchar(12), pos int) RETURNS varchar(255) CHARSET latin1
return replace(substring(substring_index(x, delim, pos), 
length(substring_index(x, delim, pos - 1)) + 1), delim, '') ;;
DELIMITER ;

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `addCharToString`(in configId int, 
in batchId int, in srcField varchar(10),
in fieldA varchar(10), in fieldB varchar(10), in con1 varchar(255), 
in con2 varchar(255), in macroId int, in foroutboundProcessing boolean, in passClear int, in transactionId int)
proc_main:begin

call setInboundOutBoundTables (foroutboundProcessing);
select @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable
into @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable;

call getFinalStatusIds;
select @finalStatusIds into @finalStatusIds;

-- we build sql here 

if (transactionId = 0) then
set @stmt = concat("update ", @translatedTable," set ",fieldA,
" = concat(substring(",fieldA,", 1,",con2,"-1), '",con1,"', substring(",fieldA,", ",con2,",(length(",fieldA,")))) where ", @transactionTable ,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (",@finalStatusIds,"));");
END if;

if (transactionId != 0) then
set @stmt = concat("update ", @translatedTable," set ",fieldA,
" = concat(substring(",fieldA,", 1,",con2,"-1), '",con1,"', substring(",fieldA,", ",con2, 
",(length(",fieldA,")))) where ", @transactionTable ,"Id = ",transactionId, ";");
END if;

PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
EXECUTE stmt;-- execute

-- we check pass /clear
if (passClear = 2) THEN
BEGIN
-- not sure how to pass clear this
END;
END IF;
-- see if we want to return something
select '';

end proc_main ;;

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `appendPrependString`(in configId int, 
in batchId int, in srcField varchar(10),
in fieldA varchar(10), in fieldB varchar(10), in con1 varchar(255), 
in con2 varchar(255), in macroId int, in foroutboundProcessing boolean, in passClear int, in transactionId int)
proc_main:begin

call setInboundOutBoundTables (foroutboundProcessing);
select @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable
into @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable;

call getFinalStatusIds;
select @finalStatusIds into @finalStatusIds;

/** 
fieldA - which field would you like to append and / or prepend?
con1 - what string would you like to prepend?
con2 - what string would you like to append?
**/
-- we build sql here 



if (transactionId = 0) then
set @stmt = concat("update ", @translatedTable," set ",fieldA,
" = concat('", con1, "', ", fieldA, ", '", con2,"') where ", @transactionTable ,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (",@finalStatusIds,"));");
END if;

if (transactionId != 0) then
set @stmt = concat("update ", @translatedTable," set ",fieldA,
" = concat('", con1, "', ", fieldA, ", '", con2,"') where ", @transactionTable ,"Id = ",transactionId, ";");
END if;

PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
EXECUTE stmt;-- execute

-- we check pass /clear
if (passClear = 2) THEN
BEGIN
-- not sure how to pass clear this
END;
END IF;
-- see if we want to return something
select '';

end proc_main ;;

/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;

/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `closeOutReferral`(in configId int, 
in batchId int, in srcField varchar(10),
in fieldA varchar(10), in fieldB varchar(255), in con1 varchar(255), 
in con2 varchar(10), in macroId int, in foroutboundProcessing boolean, in passClear int, in transactionId int)
proc_main:begin

call setInboundOutBoundTables (foroutboundProcessing);
select @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable
into @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable;

-- Need to get the value of the srcField to see what the referral status is set to
begin

if(transactionId > 0) then
	set @stmt = concat("select ", " ", srcField, " INTO @referralStatus from ", @translatedTable, " where transactionInId = ", transactionId);

	PREPARE stmt1 FROM @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt1;
	DEALLOCATE PREPARE stmt1;

	if(@referralStatus = 2) then

		BEGIN 
			set @stmt = concat("select transactionInId INTO @transactionInId from transactionTarget where id = (select transactionTargetId from transactionIn where id = ", transactionId, " )");
			
			PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
			EXECUTE stmt;
			DEALLOCATE PREPARE stmt;

			set @stmt = concat("update transactionIn set messageStatus = 2 where id = ", @transactionInId);
			PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
			EXECUTE stmt;

		END;

	END if;

	
else 

	begin

	DECLARE transId int;
	DECLARE done INT DEFAULT FALSE;
	
	DECLARE cur CURSOR for select id from transactionin where batchId = batchId;
	DECLARE CONTINUE HANDLER FOR NOT FOUND SET done = TRUE;
	
	OPEN cur;

	read_loop: LOOP

		IF done THEN
			LEAVE read_loop;
		END IF;

		FETCH cur INTO transId;
		
		if(transId > 0) then
			set @stmt = concat("select ", " ", srcField, " INTO @referralStatus from ", @translatedTable, " where transactionInId = ", transId);

			PREPARE stmt1 FROM @stmt;
			EXECUTE stmt1;
			DEALLOCATE PREPARE stmt1;

			if(@referralStatus = 2) then

				BEGIN 
					set @stmt = concat("select transactionInId INTO @transactionInId from transactionTarget where id = (select transactionTargetId from transactionIn where id = ", transId, " )");
					
					PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
					EXECUTE stmt;
					DEALLOCATE PREPARE stmt;

					set @stmt = concat("update transactionIn set messageStatus = 2 where id = ", @transactionInId);
					PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
					EXECUTE stmt;

				END;

			END if;
		end if;

	END LOOP;
	CLOSE cur; 

	end;

end if;


END;

select '';

END proc_main ;;
DELIMITER ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = @saved_sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = @saved_cs_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = @saved_cs_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = @saved_col_connection */ ;
/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `concatFieldToList` */;

/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `concatFieldToList`(in configId int, 
in batchId int, in srcField varchar(10),
in fieldA varchar(10), in fieldB varchar(10), in con1 varchar(255), 
in con2 varchar(255), in macroId int, in foroutboundProcessing boolean, in passClear int, in transactionId int)
proc_main:begin

-- sample usage CALL `healthelink`.`concatFieldToList`(34, 8, 'F255', 'F255', '0', '^^^^^', '3,4,5,6,8,1', 35,false, 2, 0);
/**
this procedure concats fields in Con2  with delimiter con1 and replaces fieldNo in fieldA
**/


call setInboundOutBoundTables (foroutboundProcessing);
select @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable
into @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable;

call getFinalStatusIds;
select @finalStatusIds into @finalStatusIds;

set @fields = concat('F', replace(replace(con2, ' ', ''), ',', ',F'));
set @sql = concat("concat_ws('",con1,"', " , @fields , ")");

if (transactionId = 0) then
	BEGIN
		set @stmt = concat("update " ,@translatedTable,  " set ", srcField, " = ", @sql , 
		" where " , @transactionTable, "Id in (select id from ", 
		@transactionTable, " where configId = ", configId, " and ", @batchIdType, " = ",batchId, 
		" and statusId not in (", @finalStatusIds, "));");
	end;
end if;


if (transactionId != 0) then
	BEGIN
		set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ", srcField," = ", @sql , " where ", @transactionTable,"Id = ", transactionId, ";");
	end;
end if;
/** **/
PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
EXECUTE stmt;-- execute

select '';

end proc_main ;;
DELIMITER ;

/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = @saved_cs_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = @saved_cs_results */ ;

/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;

/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;

/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = 'STRICT_TRANS_TABLES,NO_ENGINE_SUBSTITUTION' */ ;
DELIMITER ;;
CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `getConfigToFromFieldNo`(in cInId int, in cOutId int)
proc_main:begin

drop TEMPORARY TABLE if exists fieldAndNos;

CREATE TEMPORARY TABLE fieldAndNos as (select id, cOutId as configIdOut, cInId as configIdIn, 
fieldNo as fieldNoIn, fieldNo as fieldNoOut, saveToTableName, saveToTableCol from configurationFormFields where configId = cOutId order by fieldNoOut);

update fieldAndNos set fieldNoIn = 0;

BEGIN
 
    DECLARE v_finished INTEGER DEFAULT 0;
	DECLARE v_saveToTableName varchar(100) DEFAULT "";
	DECLARE v_saveToTableCol varchar(100) DEFAULT "";
	DECLARE v_fieldNoIn int DEFAULT 0;
	DECLARE v_fieldNoOut int DEFAULT 0;
	DECLARE v_newFieldNo int DEFAULT 0;
	DECLARE v_id int default 0;

 
    -- declare cursor for employee email
    DEClARE fieldNo_cursor CURSOR FOR 
        SELECT id, fieldNoIn, fieldNoOut, saveToTableName, saveToTableCol from fieldAndNos order by fieldNoOut;

    -- declare NOT FOUND handler
    DECLARE CONTINUE HANDLER 
        FOR NOT FOUND SET v_finished = 1;
	
    OPEN fieldNo_cursor;
	
	get_fieldNo: LOOP
		
		
        
		FETCH fieldNo_cursor INTO v_id, v_fieldNoIn, v_fieldNoOut, v_saveToTableName, v_saveToTableCol;
 
        IF v_finished = 1 THEN 
            LEAVE get_fieldNo;
        END IF;
	
	
        -- find fieldNo and update
	if  (v_id > 1) then
		set v_newFieldNo = 0;
		
		select count(fieldNo) into v_newFieldNo from configurationFormFields where configId = cInId 
		and saveToTableName = v_saveToTableName and saveToTableCol = v_saveToTableCol order by fieldNo limit 1;
		
		if (v_newFieldNo > 0) then
			select fieldNo into v_newFieldNo from configurationFormFields where configId = cInId 
			and saveToTableName = v_saveToTableName and saveToTableCol = v_saveToTableCol order by fieldNo limit 1;
			update fieldAndNos set fieldNoIn = v_newFieldNo where id = v_id;
		end if; 
		
		
		
	end if;
	
    END LOOP get_fieldNo;
 
    CLOSE fieldNo_cursor;

	
END;

select * from fieldAndNos order by fieldNoOut;
end proc_main ;;
DELIMITER ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = @saved_sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = @saved_cs_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = @saved_cs_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = @saved_col_connection */ ;
/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `getFinalStatusIds` */;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_sql_mode       = @@sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = 'STRICT_TRANS_TABLES,NO_ENGINE_SUBSTITUTION' */ ;
DELIMITER ;;
CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `getFinalStatusIds`()
proc_main:begin

set @finalStatusIds =  '11,12,13,16';

end proc_main ;;
DELIMITER ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = @saved_sql_mode */ ;

/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `insertValidationErrors` */;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_sql_mode       = @@sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = 'STRICT_TRANS_TABLES,NO_ENGINE_SUBSTITUTION' */ ;
DELIMITER ;;
CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `insertValidationErrors`(in vtType int, in fieldNo int,
in batchUploadId int, in configId int, in transactionId int)
BEGIN

DECLARE regEx varchar(100) DEFAULT '';

CASE vtType
	WHEN 2 THEN set regEx = '^[A-Z0-9._%-]+@[A-Z0-9.-]+\.[A-Z]{2,4}$';
    WHEN 3 THEN 
		BEGIN 
			CALL `healthelink`.`stripPhoneChars`(vtType, fieldNo, batchUploadId, configId, transactionId);
			set regEx ='^[0-9]{7,11}$';
		END;
	WHEN 5 THEN set regEx = '^-?[0-9]+[.]?[0-9]*$|^-?[.][0-9]+$';
    ELSE
        BEGIN
        END;
	END 
	CASE;

IF (transactionId = 0) THEN
set @stmt = concat(
'insert into transactionInerrors (batchUploadId, transactionInId, fieldNo, errorid, configId,
validationTypeId) SELECT ', batchUploadId, ', transactionInId, ',fieldNo,',2, ',configId, ',' , vtType,'  
 FROM transactionTranslatedIn WHERE trim(F' ,fieldNo, ') not REGEXP  "', regEx, '" and F',fieldNo, ' is not null 
and length(F', fieldNO, ') != 0
and length(trim(F', fieldNO, ')) != 0
and length(REPLACE(REPLACE(F', fieldNO,' , "\n", ""), "\r", "") != 0) and configId = ', configId, ' and transactionInId 
in (select id from transactionIn where batchId = ', batchUploadId,' and configId = ', configId,' and statusId not in (11,12,13,16));'
);

BEGIN -- true
		PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
		EXECUTE stmt;
END; 
END IF;

IF (transactionId != 0) THEN

set @stmt= concat(
'insert into transactionInerrors (batchUploadId, transactionInId, fieldNo, errorid, configId, 
validationTypeId) SELECT ', batchUploadId, ', transactionInId, ',fieldNo,',2, ', configId, ',', vtType,'  
 FROM transactionTranslatedIn WHERE trim(F' ,fieldNo, ') not REGEXP  "', regEx, '" and F',fieldNo, ' is not null 
and length(F', fieldNO, ') != 0
and length(trim(F', fieldNO, ')) != 0
and length(REPLACE(REPLACE(F', fieldNO,', "\n", ""), "\r", "") != 0) and configId = ', configId, ' and transactionInId 
in (select id from transactionIn where id = ', transactionId, ');'
);

BEGIN -- true
		PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
		EXECUTE stmt;


END; 
END IF;


END ;;
DELIMITER ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = @saved_sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = @saved_cs_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = @saved_cs_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = @saved_col_connection */ ;
/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `MatchFAUpdateSF` */;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `MatchFAUpdateSF`(in configId int, 
in batchId int, in srcField varchar(10),
in fieldA varchar(10), in fieldB varchar(10), in con1 varchar(255), 
in con2 varchar(255), in macroId int, in foroutboundProcessing boolean, in passClear int, in transactionId int)
proc_main:begin

-- this SP matches FieldA with Con1 and then updates fieldB with Con2
-- this sets out table
call setInboundOutBoundTables (foroutboundProcessing);
select @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable
into @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable;

call getFinalStatusIds;
select @finalStatusIds into @finalStatusIds;
-- build our sql
if (transactionId = 0) then
	BEGIN
		set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",srcField," = '",con2,"' where ",fieldA," = '",con1,"'
		and ",@transactionTable,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
		" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (", @finalStatusIds, "));");
	END;
	END if;

if (transactionId != 0) then
	BEGIN
		set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",srcField," = '",con2,"' where ",fieldA," = '",con1,"'
		and ",@transactionTable,"Id = ", transactionId, ";");
	END;
	END if;



PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
EXECUTE stmt;-- execute

-- we check pass /clear
if (passClear = 2) THEN
BEGIN

if (transactionId = 0) then
	BEGIN
		set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",srcField," = null where ",fieldB," != '",con2,"'
and ",@transactionTable,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (", @finalStatusIds,"));");

	END;
	END if;

if (transactionId != 0) then
	BEGIN
		set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",srcField," = null where ",fieldB," != '",con2,
		"' and ",@transactionTable,"Id = ", transactionId,";");
	END;
	END if;

PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
EXECUTE stmt;-- execute
END;
END IF;

-- the only error for this is if SP bombs, no need to write in insert error logs
select '';
end proc_main ;;
DELIMITER ;

	BEGIN
	set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",fieldB," = '",con2,"' where ",fieldA," = '",con1,"'
				and ",@transactionTable,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
				" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (",@finalStatusIds ,"));");
	END;
	END if;

	" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (",@finalStatusIds,"));");
	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;-- execute
	END;
	END if;

if (transactionId != 0) then
	BEGIN
	set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",fieldB," = null where ",fieldB," != '",con2,"'
	and ",@transactionTable,"Id = ", transactionId, ";");
	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;-- execute
	END;
	END if;

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `mmddyyyytoyyyymmdd`(in configId int, 
in batchId int, in srcField varchar(10),
in fieldA varchar(10), in fieldB varchar(10), in con1 varchar(10), 
in con2 varchar(10), in macroId int, in foroutboundProcessing boolean, in passClear int, in transactionId int)
proc_main:begin

call setInboundOutBoundTables (foroutboundProcessing);
select @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable
into @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable;

call getFinalStatusIds;
select @finalStatusIds into @finalStatusIds;

if (length(fieldA) = 0) then
set fieldA = srcField;
end if;

if (length(con1) = 0) then
set con1 = "/";
end if;

-- we build sql here 

if (transactionId = 0) then
	BEGIN
		set @stmt = concat("update ", @translatedTable," set ",fieldA," = 
		concat(substring(",srcField, ", 7,4), '",con1, "',  
		substring(", srcField, ", 1,2),'",con1,"' ,substring(",srcField, ", 4,2))
		where ", @transactionTable ,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
		" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (", @finalStatusIds, "));");
	END;
	END if;

if (transactionId != 0) then
	BEGIN
		set @stmt = concat("update ", @translatedTable," set ",fieldA," = 
		concat(substring(",srcField, ", 7,4), '",con1, "',  
		substring(", srcField, ", 1,2),'",con1,"' ,substring(",srcField, ", 4,2))
		where ", @transactionTable ,"Id = ", transactionId, ";");
	END;
	END if;

PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
EXECUTE stmt;-- execute

-- we check pass /clear
if (passClear = 2) THEN
BEGIN
-- if we want to fail anything, we will set forcw to MACRO_ERROR
-- not sure how to pass clear this
END;
END IF;
-- see if we want to return something
select '';

end proc_main ;;

/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `removeTransactionTargets` */;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `removeTransactionTargets`(in configId int, 
in batchId int, in srcField varchar(10),
in fieldA varchar(10), in fieldB varchar(10), in con1 varchar(255), 
in con2 varchar(255), in macroId int, in foroutboundProcessing boolean, in passClear int, in transactionId int)
proc_main:begin

/**
fieldA - field to look for value
fieldB - not in use
con1 - value to match


This is a pre-processing target for outbound that removes the target entirely from all tables
This is a per transaction macro
transaction will fail if in transactionId  is not a valid int and java codes will handle our transaction

**/

/** the id we get will be a transactionTargetId - we need to find the transactionInId since we need to clear
all tables as if the transaction never happended
**/
set @tInId = 0;
set @tOutId = 0;
set @batchInId = 0;
set @getTInId = concat("select transactionInId, id, batchUploadId into @tInId, @tOutId, @batchInId from transactionTarget where id = "
, transactionId ," and id in (select transactionTargetId from transactionTranslatedOut where "
,fieldA," = '",con1, "' and transactionTargetId = ", transactionId,");");


prepare stmt from @getTInId;
execute stmt;

set @processStatus = 'continue';
if (@tInId > 0) then
begin

call deleteTransaction (@tInId, @tOutId);
-- we need to update the original batch count

set @batchCount = 0;
set @batchInfoSql = concat("select count(*) into @batchCount from transactionIN where batchId = ",@batchInId);

prepare stmt from @batchInfoSql;
execute stmt;

-- now we update counts

set @batchInfoSql1 = concat("update batchUploads set totalrecordcount =  ", @batchCount, " where id = ",
@batchInId);

prepare stmt from @batchInfoSql1;
execute stmt;

set @processStatus = 'stop';
end;
end if;

select @processStatus;

end proc_main ;;
DELIMITER ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = @saved_sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = @saved_cs_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = @saved_cs_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = @saved_col_connection */ ;
/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `replaceBlanksWithChars` */;

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `replaceBlanksWithChars`(in configId int, 
in batchId int, in srcField varchar(10),
in fieldA varchar(10), in fieldB varchar(10), in con1 varchar(255), 
in con2 varchar(255), in macroId int, in foroutboundProcessing boolean, in passClear int, in transactionId int)
proc_main:begin

-- this SP matches null or empty for fieldA and will replace it with con1
-- FieldA - Field you would like to replace
-- Con1 - what value would you like to replace null with

set @fieldToReplace = fieldA;
if (fieldB != 'F') then
	set @fieldToReplace = fieldB;
end if;

-- this sets out table
call setInboundOutBoundTables (foroutboundProcessing);
select @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable
into @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable;

call getFinalStatusIds;
select @finalStatusIds into @finalStatusIds;

-- build our sql
if (transactionId = 0) then
	set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",fieldA," = '" ,con1,  "' where (",@fieldToReplace, " is null  
	or length(REPLACE(REPLACE('", fieldA, "', ""\n"", """"), ""\r"", """")) = 0)and ",
	@transactionTable,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
				" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (",@finalStatusIds ,"));");
	END if;



if (transactionId != 0) then
	set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",fieldA," = '",con1, "' where (", @fieldToReplace , " is null
		or length(REPLACE(REPLACE('", fieldA, "', ""\n"", """"), ""\r"", """")) = 0)and ",
	@transactionTable,"Id = ", transactionId,";");
	END if;


	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;-- execute



-- we check pass /clear
if (passClear = 2) THEN
BEGIN
-- accessible
END;
END IF;


-- the only error for this is if SP bombs, no need to write in insert error logs
select '';
end proc_main ;;
DELIMITER ;

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `setInboundOutBoundTables`(in foroutboundProcessing boolean)
proc_main:begin

-- this SP sets the inbound / outbound tables
set @translatedTable = "transactionTranslatedIn";
set @transactionTable = "transactionIn";
set @batchTable = "batchUploads";
set @batchIdType = "batchId";
set @errorTable = "transactionInErrors";

if (foroutboundProcessing) THEN
BEGIN -- true
		set @translatedTable = "transactionTranslatedOut";
		set @transactionTable = "transactionTarget";
		set @batchTable = "batchDowloads";
		set @batchIdType = "batchDLId";
		set @errorTable = "transactionOutErrors";
END; 
END IF;

end proc_main ;;

/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;

/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;

DELIMITER ;;
CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `setSqlForConfig`(in inConfigId int, in batchUploadId int)
proc_main:begin
drop TEMPORARY TABLE if exists temp1;
CREATE TEMPORARY TABLE temp1
as (select min(fieldNo) as fieldNo, saveToTableName, savetotablecol, configId, batchUploadId
from configurationFormFields where configId = inConfigId
and saveToTableName != ''
group by savetotablecol, saveToTableName);
SELECT  batchUploadId, saveToTableName, 
group_concat(distinct savetotablecol ORDER BY fieldNo SEPARATOR ',') as savetotablecol,
group_concat( concat('F',fieldNo) ORDER BY fieldNo SEPARATOR ',') as singleValueFields, 
group_concat( concat('strSplit(F',fieldNo, ', ''^^^^^'',@valPos)') ORDER BY fieldNo SEPARATOR ',') as splitFields, 
group_concat( concat('F',fieldNo, ' like ''%^^^^^%''') ORDER BY fieldNo SEPARATOR ' or ') as checkForDelim,
configId
FROM temp1 
where configId = inConfigId
GROUP BY saveToTableName
ORDER BY saveToTableName;
end proc_main ;;
DELIMITER ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = @saved_sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = @saved_cs_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = @saved_cs_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = @saved_col_connection */ ;
/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `stripCharAtPos` */;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;

/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `stripCharAtPos`(in configId int, 
in batchId int, in srcField varchar(10), in fieldA varchar(10), in fieldB varchar(10), in con1 varchar(255), 
in con2 varchar(255), in macroId int, in foroutboundProcessing boolean, in passClear int, in transactionId int)
proc_main:begin
-- sample usage CALL `healthelink`.`stripCharAtPos`(34, 12, 'F3', 'F255', 'F', '4', '', 9875, false, 2, 0);

-- this sets out table
call setInboundOutBoundTables (foroutboundProcessing);
select @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable
into @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable;

call getFinalStatusIds;
select @finalStatusIds into @finalStatusIds;

-- fieldA - field to update, fieldA already has false
-- fieldB - field to read value from
-- conA  field position
-- conB field to match, leave blank if just dropping

set @readField = fieldA;
set @strCompare = '';

select fieldB;
if (fieldB != 'F') then
	begin 
		set @readField = fieldB;
end;
end if; 

if (length(trim(con2)) != 0) then
	begin 
		set @strCompare = concat(" and substring(", @readField, ",", con1, ", 1) = '", con2, "'");
	end;
end if; 

-- build our sql
if (transactionId = 0) then
begin

select @readField;

set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",fieldA," = concat(substring(", @readField,", 1, (", con1, "-1)), 
substring(", @readField, ", (", con1, " + 1),length(", @readField,")- ", con1,")) where length(", @readField,") >= " ,con1 , 
@strCompare, "  and ",@transactionTable,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (",@finalStatusIds ,"));");

end;
END if;


if (transactionId != 0) then

	set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",fieldA," = concat(substring(", @readField,", 1, (", con1, "-1)), 
	substring(", @readField, ", (", con1, " + 1),length(", @readField,")- ", con1,")) where length(", @readField,") >= " ,con1 , 
	@strCompare, "  and ",@transactionTable,"Id =", transactionId,";");
END if;

-- insert into formula (formula) values (@stmt);

 PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
 EXECUTE stmt;-- execute

-- we check pass /clear
if (passClear = 2) THEN
BEGIN
-- accessible
END;
END IF;


-- the only error for this is if SP bombs, no need to write in insert error logs
select '';
end proc_main ;;

if (transactionId = 0) then

/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_sql_mode       = @@sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = 'STRICT_TRANS_TABLES,NO_ENGINE_SUBSTITUTION' */ ;
DELIMITER ;;
CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `stripPhoneChars`(in vtType int, in fieldNo int,
in batchUploadId int, in configId int, in transactionId int)
BEGIN
	DECLARE varToReplace varchar(100) DEFAULT '.';
	DECLARE part1 varchar(255) DEFAULT '.';
	DECLARE part2 varchar(25) DEFAULT '.';
	
	if (transactionId = 0) then
	BEGIN
		set part1 = concat("update transactiontranslatedIn JOIN (SELECT id from transactionIn WHERE configId = ",
	  configId,"  and batchId = ", batchUploadId, " and statusId not in (11,12,13,16)) as ti ON transactiontranslatedIn.transactionInId = ti.id SET transactiontranslatedIn.F"
	  , fieldNo, " = replace(F", fieldNo, ", '");
	END;
	END if;

	if (transactionId != 0) then
	BEGIN
	  set part1 = concat("update transactiontranslatedIn JOIN (SELECT id from transactionIn WHERE id = ",
	  transactionId, ") as ti ON transactiontranslatedIn.transactionInId = ti.id SET transactiontranslatedIn.F"
	  , fieldNo, " = replace(F", fieldNo, ", '");
	END;
	END if;

	
	set part2 = "', '');";
	set @stmt = concat(part1, varToReplace, part2);
  	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;

	set varToReplace = '-';
	set @stmt = concat(part1, varToReplace, part2);
	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;

	set varToReplace = ')';
	set @stmt = concat(part1, varToReplace, part2);
	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;

	set varToReplace = '(';
	set @stmt = concat(part1, varToReplace, part2);
	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;

	set varToReplace = ' ';
	set @stmt = concat(part1, varToReplace, part2);
	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;

 END ;;
DELIMITER ;

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `trimField`(in configId int, 
in batchId int, in srcField varchar(10),
in fieldA varchar(10), in fieldB varchar(10), in con1 varchar(255), 
in con2 varchar(255), in macroId int, in foroutboundProcessing boolean, in passClear int, in transactionId int)
proc_main:begin

-- this SP matches FieldA with Con1 and then updates fieldB with Con2
-- this sets out table
call setInboundOutBoundTables (foroutboundProcessing);
select @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable
into @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable;

call getFinalStatusIds;
select @finalStatusIds into @finalStatusIds;

-- build our sql
if (transactionId = 0) then
	set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",fieldA, " = TRIM(REPLACE(REPLACE(" , fieldA , ", '\\n', ''), '\\r', '')) where ",@transactionTable,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
				" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (",@finalStatusIds ,"));");
	END if;

if (transactionId != 0) then
	set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",fieldA, " = Trim(REPLACE(REPLACE(" , fieldA , 
	", '\\n', ''), '\\r', '')) where ",@transactionTable,"Id = ",transactionId, ";");
	END if;

PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
EXECUTE stmt;-- execute

-- we check pass /clear
if (passClear = 2) THEN
BEGIN
-- accessible
END;
END IF;


-- the only error for this is if SP bombs, no need to write in insert error logs
select '';
end proc_main ;;

proc_main:begin

/** 
This procedure take a string in yyyymmddhhmmss format and convert it into yyyy-mm-dd hh:mm:ss. 
"-" can be "/" or "." or character of choice by user
fieldA will be field to convert
fieldB is not in use
con1 will be character of choice
con2 is not in use
**/

call setInboundOutBoundTables (foroutboundProcessing);
select @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable
into @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable;

call getFinalStatusIds;
select @finalStatusIds into @finalStatusIds;

-- we build sql here 
if (con1 = '') then
set con1 = '-';
end if;

if (transactionId = 0) then
set @stmt = concat("update ", @translatedTable," set ",fieldA,
" = concat(substring(", fieldA,", 1, 4), '",con1,"', substring(",fieldA,", 5,2), '",con1,"', substring(",fieldA,", 7,2), ' ', substring(",fieldA,", 9,2), ':', substring(",fieldA,", 11,2), ':', substring(",fieldA,", 13,2))
 where ", @transactionTable ,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (",@finalStatusIds,"));");


END if;

if (transactionId != 0) then
set @stmt = concat("update ", @translatedTable," set ",fieldA,
" = concat(substring(", fieldA,", 1, 4), '",con1,"', substring(",fieldA,", 5,2), '",con1,"', substring(",fieldA,", 7,2), ' ', substring(",fieldA,", 9,2), ':', substring(",fieldA,", 11,2), ':', substring(",fieldA,", 13,2)) 
where ", @transactionTable ,"Id = ",transactionId, ";");
END if;


PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
EXECUTE stmt;-- execute

-- we check pass /clear
if (passClear = 2) THEN
BEGIN
-- not sure how to pass clear this
END;
END IF;
-- see if we want to return something
select '';

end proc_main ;;

in fieldA varchar(10), in fieldB varchar(10), in con1 varchar(10), 
in con2 varchar(10), in macroId int, in foroutboundProcessing boolean, in passClear int, in transactionId int)
proc_main:begin

set fieldA = srcField;
end if;

if (length(con1) = 0) then
set con1 = "/";
end if;

-- we build sql here 
if (transactionId = 0) then
	BEGIN
		set @stmt = concat("update ", @translatedTable," set ",fieldA," = 
		concat(substring(",srcField, ", 6,2), '",con1, "',  
		substring(", srcField, ", 9,2),'",con1,"' ,substring(",srcField, ", 1,4))
		where ", @transactionTable ,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
		" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (",@finalStatusIds,"));");
	END;
	END if;

if (transactionId != 0) then
	BEGIN
		set @stmt = concat("update ", @translatedTable," set ",fieldA," = 
		concat(substring(",srcField, ", 6,2), '",con1, "',  
		substring(", srcField, ", 9,2),'",con1,"' ,substring(",srcField, ", 1,4))

	END if;
